Directory containing MP4 files\nTRANSCRIPT_DIR = \"/Users/steven/Movies/poject2025/mp4/transcript\"  # Directory to save transcripts\nANALYSIS_DIR = \"/Users/steven/Movies/poject2025/mp4/analysis\"  # Directory to save the analysis files\n\n# Create output directories if they don't exist\nos.makedirs(TRANSCRIPT_DIR, exist_ok=True)\nos.makedirs(ANALYSIS_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Function to split the video into sections using ffmpeg\ndef split_video_to_segments(video_path, segment_length=300):\n    \"\"\"Split the video into smaller segments.\"\"\"\n    video_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(video_path))[0]\n    output_dir = os.path.join(VIDEO_DIR, video_name + \"_segments\")\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # Using ffmpeg to split the video into smaller segments\n    command = [\n        \"ffmpeg\", \"-i\", video_path, \"-c\", \"copy\", \"-map\", \"0\",\n        \"-segment_time\", str(segment_length), \"-f\", \"segment\", \n        \"-reset_timestamps\", \"1\", os.path.join(output_dir, video_name + \"_%03d.mp4\")\n    ]\n    subprocess.run(command)\n\n    # List the generated segments\n    segments = sorted([os.path.join(output_dir, f) for f in os.listdir(output_dir) if f.endswith('.mp4')])\n    return segments\n\n# Function to transcribe video segments using Whisper\ndef transcribe_video_segment(file_path):\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as video_file:\n        transcript_data = openai.Audio.transcribe(\"whisper-1\", video_file, response_format=\"verbose_json\")\n\n        # Build the transcript with timestamps\n        transcript_with_timestamps = []\n        for segment in transcript_data['segments']:\n            start_time = segment['start']\n            end_time = segment['end']\n            text = segment['text']\n            transcript_with_timestamps.append(f\"{format_timestamp(start_time)} -- {format_timestamp(end_time)}: {text}\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(transcript_with_timestamps)\n\n# Helper function to format timestamps\ndef format_timestamp(seconds):\n    minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n    seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n    return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n# Function to analyze the transcript for a section\ndef analyze_text_for_section(text, section_number):\n    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n        model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n        messages=[\n            {\"role\": \"system\",\n                \"content\": (\n                    \"You are an expert in multimedia analysis and storytelling. Consider every nuance and provide insights into how audio and visual elements, editing, and special effects contribute to the overall experience.\"\n                )\n            },\n            {\n                \"role\": \"user\",\n                \"content\": (\n                    f\"Provide an in-depth analysis for {section_number}. Please address the following aspects:\\n\"\n                    \"1. **Central Themes and Messages**: What are the primary themes, and how complex are the underlying messages?\\n\"\n                    \"2. **Emotional Tone**: Describe the range of emotions conveyed. Identify key turning points and their significance.\\n\"\n                    \"4. **Creator’s Intent and Vision**: What deeper message or purpose might the creator be conveying? How do multimedia elements support this intent?\\n\"\n                    \"5. **Technical and Artistic Elements**: Analyze the use of cinematography, editing, sound design, and any special effects. How do these technical choices enhance the storytelling?\\n\"\n                    \"6. **Audience Impact and Engagement**: Evaluate how effectively the content captures and maintains audience attention. What makes it engaging?\\n\"\n                    \"\\nTranscript:\\n\" + text)}\n        ],\n        max_tokens=1000,\n        temperature=0.7\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].message['content'].strip()\n\n# Main function to process large videos in sections\ndef process_video_by_section(video_file, segment_length=300):\n    # Split video into smaller segments\n    segments = split_video_to_segments(video_file, segment_length)\n\n    # Process each segment\n    for index, segment in enumerate(segments):\n        section_number = index + 1\n        print(f\"Processing Section {section_number}: {segment}\")\n\n        # Step 1: Transcribe the segment\n        transcript = transcribe_video_segment(segment)\n        transcript_file_path = os.path.join(TRANSCRIPT_DIR, f\"section_{section_number}_transcript.txt\")\n        with open(transcript_file_path, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(transcript)\n        print(f\"Transcription saved for Section {section_number} at {transcript_file_path}\")\n\n        # Step 2: Analyze the segment's transcript\n        analysis = analyze_text_for_section(transcript, section_number)\n        analysis_file_path = os.path.join(ANALYSIS_DIR, f\"section_{section_number}_analysis.txt\")\n        with open(analysis_file_path, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(analysis)\n        print(f\"Analysis saved for Section {section_number} at {analysis_file_path}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    import sys\n    video_file = sys.argv[1]  # Path to the MP4 file\n    process_video_by_section(video_file, segment_length=300)  # Break into 5-minute sections"

            "content": "# WhisperTranscriber\n# src: https://github.com/VimWei/WhisperTranscriber\n# Implement Whisper's basic parameter configuration\n# Implement parameter control of srt output, so that verbatim srt can be achieved\n    # max_line_width，max_line_count，max_words_per_line\n# Realize free switching of srt line breaking control: manual or automatic\n\nimport whisper\nimport the\nimport json\nimport yaml\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef load_config(config_file='config.yaml'):\n    \"\"\"Load configuration file\"\"\"\n    with open(config_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        return yaml.safe_load(f)\n\ndef get_media_files(config):\n    \"\"\"Get the list of media files to be processed\"\"\"\n    input_dir = config['input']['directory']\n    formats = config['input']['formats']\n    specific_files = config['input']['specific_files']\n\n    # Make sure the input directory exists\n    if not os.path.exists(input_dir):\n        os.makedirs(input_dir)\n        print(f\"Created input directory: {input_dir}\")\n        return []\n\n    # If specific files are specified, only those files will be processed\n    if specific_files:\n        return [os.path.join(input_dir, f) for f in specific_files \n                if os.path.exists(os.path.join(input_dir, f))]\n\n    # Otherwise process all supported formats in the directory\n    media_files = []\n    for format in formats:\n        media_files.extend(\n            str(p) for p in Path(input_dir).glob(f\"*{format}\")\n        )\n    \n    return sorted(media_files)\n\ndef transcribe_audio(config_file='config.yaml'):\n    \"\"\"Use the configuration file's transcription function\"\"\"\n    # Load configuration\n    config = load_config(config_file)\n    \n    # Get the media file to be processed\n    media_files = get_media_files(config)\n    \n    if not media_files:\n        print(f\"No media files found in {config['input']['directory']}\")\n        print(f\"Supported formats: {', '.join(config['input']['formats'])}\")\n        return\n\n    print(f\"Found {len(media_files)} files to process:\")\n    for file in media_files:\n        print(f\"  - {os.path.basename(file)}\")\n    print()\n\n    # Load the model\n    model = whisper.load_model(\n        config['model']['name'],\n        device=config['model']['device']\n    )\n\n    for audio in media_files:\n        print(f\"Processing: {os.path.basename(audio)}\")\n        # Get the file name (remove the extension)\n        base_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(audio))[0]\n\n        # Using the transcribe function\n        result = model.transcribe(\n            audio,\n            language=config['transcription']['language'],\n            task=config['transcription']['task'],\n            temperature=config['transcription']['temperature'],\n            best_of=config['transcription']['best_of'],\n            beam_size=config['transcription']['beam_size'],\n            patience=config['transcription']['patience'],\n            length_penalty=config['transcription']['length_penalty'],\n            suppress_tokens=config['transcription']['suppress_tokens'],\n            initial_prompt=config['transcription']['initial_prompt'],\n            condition_on_previous_text=config['transcription']['condition_on_previous_text'],\n            fp16=config['model']['fp16'],\n            word_timestamps=config['transcription']['word_timestamps'],\n            verbose=config['output']['verbose'],\n        )\n\n        # Processing output\n        formats = config['output']['format'] if config['output']['format'] != 'all' else [\"txt\", \"vtt\", \"srt\", \"json\"]\n\n        for fmt in formats:\n            output_file = os.path.join(config['output']['directory'], f\"{base_name}.{fmt}\")\n            if fmt == \"txt\":\n                with open(output_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    f.write(result[\"text\"])\n            elif fmt == \"srt\":\n                # Manually process SRT output\n                with open(output_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    if config['srt']['use_default_line_breaks']:\n                        write_srt_with_default_line_breaks(result, f)\n                    else:\n                        write_srt_with_word_timestamps(\n                            result, \n                            f,\n                            config['srt']['max_line_width'],\n                            config['srt']['max_line_count'],\n                            config['srt']['max_words_per_line']\n                        )\n            elif fmt == \"vtt\":\n                with open(output_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    writer = whisper.utils.WriteVTT(config['output']['directory'])\n                    writer.write_result(result, f)\n            elif fmt == \"json\":\n                with open(output_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n                    json.dump(result, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)\n\n        if config['output']['verbose']:\n            print(f\"Transcription complete for {audio}. Output saved to {config['output']['directory']}\")\n\ndef write_srt_with_word_timestamps(result, file, max_line_width=None, max_line_count=None, max_words_per_line=None):\n    # Initialize variables\n    line_index = 1\n    current_line = \"\"\n    current_line_start = None\n    current_line_end = None\n    words_in_line = 0\n\n    for segment in result[\"segments\"]:\n        for word in segment[\"words\"]:\n            # Check if line break is needed\n            if (max_line_width and len(current_line) + len(word[\"word\"]) + 1 > max_line_width) or \\\n               (max_words_per_line and words_in_line >= max_words_per_line) or \\\n               (max_line_count and line_index >= max_line_count):\n                # Write the current line\n                if current_line_start is not None and current_line_end is not None:\n                    print(f\"{line_index}\\n{format_timestamp(current_line_start)} --> {format_timestamp(current_line_end)}\\n{current_line.strip()}\\n\", file=file)\n                # Reset the current line\n                line_index += 1\n                current_line = \"\"\n                current_line_start = None\n                current_line_end = None\n                words_in_line = 0\n\n            # Update the start and end times of the row\n            if current_line_start is None:\n                current_line_start = word[\"start\"]\n            current_line_end = word[\"end\"]\n\n            # Append words\n            current_line += word[\"word\"] + \" \"\n            words_in_line += 1\n\n    # Write the last line\n    if current_line:\n        if current_line_start is not None and current_line_end is not None:\n            print(f\"{line_index}\\n{format_timestamp(current_line_start)} --> {format_timestamp(current_line_end)}\\n{current_line.strip()}\\n\", file=file)\n\ndef write_srt_with_default_line_breaks(result, file):\n    for segment in result[\"segments\"]:\n        start = format_timestamp(segment[\"start\"])\n        end = format_timestamp(segment[\"end\"])\n        text = segment[\"text\"].strip().replace(\"-->\", \"->\")\n        print(f\"{segment['id']}\\n{start} --> {end}\\n{text}\\n\", file=file)\n\ndef format_timestamp(seconds: float):\n    milliseconds = int(seconds * 1000)\n    hours = milliseconds // 3600000\n    minutes = (milliseconds % 3600000) // 60000\n    seconds = (milliseconds % 60000) // 1000\n    milliseconds = milliseconds % 1000\n    return f\"{hours:02d}:{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d},{milliseconds:03d}\"\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    transcribe_audio()"

            "content": "import os\nimport time\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom PIL import Image, UnidentifiedImageError\nimport csv\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\n# 🚀 Constants\nTARGET_DPI = 300\nUPSCALE_MULTIPLIER = 2  # How much to enlarge small images\nBATCH_SIZE = 50\nPAUSE_DURATION = 3  # Just for dramatic effect 🎭\nSIZE_THRESHOLD_MB = 9  # The Holy Grail of size rules\n\n# 📜 Log Data\nlog_data = []\n\n# 🏆 Ask the user for the processing mode\ndef get_user_choice():\n    print(\"\\n🎯 Choose Processing Mode:\")\n    print(\"1️⃣ Only resize images 9MB+ (Skip smaller ones)\")\n    print(\"2️⃣ Resize 9MB+ & upscale anything smaller\")\n    print(\"3️⃣ Only upscale images below 9MB (Ignore large ones)\")\n    \n    while True:\n        choice = input(\"\\n🔹 Enter 1, 2, or 3: \").strip()\n        if choice in (\"1\", \"2\", \"3\"):\n            return int(choice)\n        print(\"❌ Invalid choice! Please enter 1, 2, or 3.\")\n\n# 🖨️ Apply 300 DPI\ndef apply_dpi(im, output_path):\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=95)\n\n# 🔻 Resize images larger than 9MB\ndef resize_image(im, output_path):\n    print(f\"📉 Resizing image to reduce file size...\")\n\n    quality = 95  # Start with high quality\n    while quality > 10:  # Don't go below 10, because nobody likes pixel soup\n        im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=quality)\n        file_size_mb = os.path.getsize(output_path) / (1024 ** 2)\n        if file_size_mb <= SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB:\n            print(f\"✅ Resized successfully! New Size: {file_size_mb:.2f} MB\")\n            return\n        quality -= 5  # Reduce quality until it fits\n\n    print(f\"⚠️ Could not shrink below {file_size_mb:.2f} MB, keeping best effort.\")\n\n# 🔺 Upscale images smaller than 9MB\ndef upscale_image(im, output_path):\n    print(f\"📈 Upscaling image to meet quality standards...\")\n\n    new_width = im.width * UPSCALE_MULTIPLIER\n    new_height = im.height * UPSCALE_MULTIPLIER\n\n    im = im.resize((new_width, new_height), Image.LANCZOS)\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=95)\n    print(f\"✅ Upscaled successfully to {new_width}x{new_height}!\")\n\n# 🖼️ Process a batch of images based on user choice\ndef process_batch(batch, root, mode):\n    for file in tqdm(batch, desc=\"✨ Processing images ✨\", unit=\"file\"):\n        file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n        file_ext = file.lower().split('.')[-1]\n\n        if file_ext not in ('jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'webp'):\n            print(f\"⚠️ Skipping {file}: Unsupported format.\")\n            continue  \n\n        try:\n            im = Image.open(file_path)\n            file_size_mb = os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024 ** 2)\n\n            temp_file = os.path.join(root, f\"processed_{file}\")\n\n            print(f\"\\n📂 Processing: {file} ({file_size_mb:.2f} MB)\")\n\n            if mode == 1 and file_size_mb < SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB:\n                print(f\"⏭️ Skipping {file} (Too small for resizing)\")\n                continue\n\n            # Resize if it's 9MB+ and user chose mode 1 or 2\n            if file_size_mb >= SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB and mode in (1, 2):\n                print(f\"🔻 Shrinking file (TOO BIG!)...\")\n                resize_image(im, temp_file)\n\n            # Upscale if it's below 9MB and user chose mode 2 or 3\n            elif file_size_mb < SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB and mode in (2, 3):\n                print(f\"🔺 Enlarging file (TOO SMALL!)...\")\n                upscale_image(im, temp_file)\n\n            os.replace(temp_file, file_path)  # Overwrite original\n\n            log_data.append({\n                \"File\": file,\n                \"Original Size (MB)\": round(file_size_mb, 2),\n                \"Final Size (MB)\": round(os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024 ** 2), 2),\n                \"Status\": \"Processed ✅\"\n            })\n\n        except UnidentifiedImageError:\n            print(f\"❌ ERROR: Cannot process {file}. Unrecognized format!\")\n            log_data.append({\"File\": file, \"Status\": \"Error - Unidentified Image\"})\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"❌ ERROR processing {file}: {str(e)}\")\n            log_data.append({\"File\": file, \"Status\": f\"Error - {str(e)}\"})\n\n# 📦 Process all images in a directory\ndef process_images(source_directory, mode):\n    batch = []\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_directory):\n        for file in files:\n            batch.append(file)\n            if len(batch) >= BATCH_SIZE:\n                process_batch(batch, root, mode)\n                batch = []\n                time.sleep(PAUSE_DURATION)  # ⏳ Adds suspense\n\n        if batch:\n            process_batch(batch, root, mode)\n\n# 📜 Write log to CSV with Auto-Generated Name\ndef write_log(source_directory):\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(source_directory))  # Get the folder name\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d_%H%M')  # Format: YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM\n    output_file = os.path.join(source_directory, f\"{folder_name}_{timestamp}.csv\")\n\n    fieldnames = [\"File\", \"Original Size (MB)\", \"Final Size (MB)\", \"Status\"]\n    \n    with open(output_file, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as csv_file:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerows(log_data)\n\n    print(f\"📜 Log saved as: {output_file}\")\n\n# 🚀 Main function\ndef main():\n    print(\"🔥 Welcome to the Ultimate Image Resizer & Upscaler 🔥\")\n    source_directory = input(\"📂 Enter the path to the source directory: \").strip()\n\n    if not os.path.isdir(source_directory):\n        print(\"🚨 ERROR: Source directory does not exist!\")\n        return\n\n    mode = get_user_choice()  # Ask the user for mode selection\n    process_images(source_directory, mode)\n    write_log(source_directory)\n\n    print(\"\\n🎉 All images processed successfully! 🎊\")\n    print(\"📜 A detailed log has been saved.\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

\"garment-dyed t-shirt\": [\"premium look\", \"trendy\", \"youth appeal\"],\n        \"hooded sweatshirt\": [\"cozy\", \"seasonal favorite\", \"customizable\"],\n        \"scented candle\": [\"relaxation\", \"premium home decor\", \"giftable\"],\n        \"tote bag\": [\"eco-friendly\", \"practical\", \"ideal for custom graphics\"],\n        \"matte canvas\": [\"artistic\", \"premium home decor\", \"custom prints\"],\n        \"plush blanket\": [\"soft tones\", \"comfort\", \"perfect for gifts\"],\n    }\n}\n\n# Mockup recommendations\nMOCKUP_GUIDE = {\n    \"hoodie\": \"4-6 (front, back, lifestyle shots, close-ups)\",\n    \"t-shirt\": \"4-6 (front, back, lifestyle shots, close-ups)\",\n    \"tote bag\": \"3-5 (both sides, lifestyle shots)\",\n    \"phone case\": \"3-4 (front, angled, lifestyle shots)\",\n    \"sticker\": \"2-3 (detailed, lifestyle, on products)\",\n    \"candle\": \"3-4 (top, side, lifestyle shots)\",\n    \"plush blanket\": \"3-5 (folded, spread out, lifestyle shots)\",\n    \"ceramic mug\": \"3-5 (both sides, top view, lifestyle shots)\",\n    \"matte canvas\": \"3-5 (angled, wall-mounted, close-ups)\"\n}\n\n# Get dominant color from image\ndef get_dominant_color(image_path):\n    img = Image.open(image_path).resize((50, 50))  # Downsample for faster processing\n    img_array = np.array(img).reshape(-1, 3)\n    unique, counts = np.unique(img_array, axis=0, return_counts=True)\n    dominant_color = unique[counts.argmax()]  # Most common color\n    return tuple(dominant_color)\n\n# Detect text from image using OCR\ndef detect_text(image_path):\n    img = cv2.imread(image_path)\n    gray = cv2.cvtColor(img, cv2.COLOR_BGR2GRAY)\n    text = pytesseract.image_to_string(gray)\n    return text.strip() if text else None\n\n# Suggest product type based on platform, colors, and text\ndef suggest_product(platform, dominant_color, text):\n    r, g, b = dominant_color\n    category = \"unknown\"\n\n    if text:\n        category = \"sticker\" if len(text) < 50 else \"t-shirt\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"ceramic mug\"\n\n    elif r > g and r > b:\n        category = \"hoodie\" if platform == \"tiktok\" else \"tote bag\"\n\n    elif g > r and g > b:\n        category = \"candle\"\n\n    elif b > r and b > g:\n        category = \"phone case\"\n\n    elif r > 200 and g > 200 and b > 200:\n        category = \"plush blanket\"\n\n    return category\n\n# Process batch of images\ndef process_batch(batch, root, platform):\n    csv_data = []\n    for file in tqdm(batch, desc=\"✨ Processing Files ✨\", unit=\"file\"):\n        file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n        file_ext = file.lower().split('.')[-1]\n\n        if file_ext not in ('jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'webp'):\n            print(f\"⚠️ Skipping {file}: Unsupported format.\")\n            continue\n\n        try:\n            dominant_color = get_dominant_color(file_path)\n            text_detected = detect_text(file_path)\n            product_category = suggest_product(platform, dominant_color, text_detected)\n\n            csv_data.append({\n                \"Platform\": platform.capitalize(),\n                \"File\": file,\n                \"Product\": product_category,\n                \"Category\": product_category,\n                \"Features\": \", \".join(PLATFORMS[platform].get(product_category, [])),\n                \"Mockup Recommendation\": MOCKUP_GUIDE.get(product_category, \"N/A\")\n            })\n        except UnidentifiedImageError:\n            print(f\"❌ Skipping {file}: Unidentified Image Format!\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"❌ Error processing {file}: {e}\")\n\n    return csv_data\n\n# Process images in directory\ndef process_images(source_directory, platform):\n    csv_rows = []\n    batch = []\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_directory):\n        for file in files:\n            batch.append(file)\n            if len(batch) >= BATCH_SIZE:\n                csv_rows.extend(process_batch(batch, root, platform))\n                batch = []\n                time.sleep(PAUSE_DURATION)\n\n        if batch:\n            csv_rows.extend(process_batch(batch, root, platform))\n    \n    return csv_rows\n\n# Write processed data to CSV\ndef write_csv(source_directory, csv_rows):\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(source_directory))\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d_%H%M')\n    output_file = os.path.join(source_directory, f\"{folder_name}_organized_{timestamp}.csv\")\n\n    with open(output_file, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as csv_file:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=CSV_FIELDS)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerows(csv_rows)\n\n    print(f\"📜 CSV saved as: {output_file}\")\n\n# Main Function\ndef main():\n    print(\"🔥 Welcome to the Printify Organizer 🔥\")\n    source_directory = input(\"📂 Enter the path to the source directory: \").strip()\n\n    print(\"\\n🎯 Choose Platform:\")\n    print(\"1️⃣ Etsy\")\n    print(\"2️⃣ TikTok\")\n    platform_choice = input(\"\\n🔹 Enter 1 or 2: \").strip()\n    platform = \"etsy\" if platform_choice == \"1\" else \"tiktok\" if platform_choice == \"2\" else None\n\n    if not platform:\n        print(\"❌ Invalid platform choice! Exiting.\")\n        return\n\n    if not os.path.isdir(source_directory):\n        print(\"🚨 ERROR: Source directory does not exist!\")\n        return\n\n    csv_rows = process_images(source_directory, platform)\n    write_csv(source_directory, csv_rows)\n\n    print(\"\\n🎉 All files processed and organized successfully! 🎊\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

Directory containing MP4 files\nTRANSCRIPT_DIR = \"/Users/steven/Movies/2025/mp4/transcribe\"  # Directory to save transcripts\nANALYSIS_DIR = \"/Users/steven/Movies/2025/mp4/analysis\"  # Directory to save the analysis files\n\n# Create output directories if they don't exist\nos.makedirs(TRANSCRIPT_DIR, exist_ok=True)\nos.makedirs(ANALYSIS_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Function to split the video into sections using ffmpeg\ndef split_video_to_segments(video_path, segment_length=300):\n    \"\"\"Split the video into smaller segments.\"\"\"\n    video_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(video_path))[0]\n    output_dir = os.path.join(VIDEO_DIR, video_name + \"_segments\")\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # Using ffmpeg to split the video into smaller segments\n    command = [\n        \"ffmpeg\", \"-i\", video_path, \"-c\", \"copy\", \"-map\", \"0\",\n        \"-segment_time\", str(segment_length), \"-f\", \"segment\", \n        \"-reset_timestamps\", \"1\", os.path.join(output_dir, video_name + \"_%03d.mp4\")\n    ]\n    subprocess.run(command)\n\n    # List the generated segments\n    segments = sorted([os.path.join(output_dir, f) for f in os.listdir(output_dir) if f.endswith('.mp4')])\n    return segments\n\n# Function to transcribe video segments using Whisper\ndef transcribe_video_segment(file_path):\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as video_file:\n        transcript_data = openai.Audio.transcribe(\"whisper-1\", video_file, response_format=\"verbose_json\")\n\n        # Build the transcript with timestamps\n        transcript_with_timestamps = []\n        for segment in transcript_data['segments']:\n            start_time = segment['start']\n            end_time = segment['end']\n            text = segment['text']\n            transcript_with_timestamps.append(f\"{format_timestamp(start_time)} -- {format_timestamp(end_time)}: {text}\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(transcript_with_timestamps)\n\n# Helper function to format timestamps\ndef format_timestamp(seconds):\n    minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n    seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n    return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n# Function to analyze the transcript for a section\ndef analyze_text_for_section(text, section_number):\n    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n        model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n        messages=[\n            {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a language and music expert. Your goal is to deeply analyze song lyrics to identify the core context, emotional content, and meaning. Pay attention to the emotional tone, the narrative arc, and any underlying themes or messages that the artist is conveying.\"},\n            {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Analyze the following song transcript to extract: (1) main themes, (2) emotions, (3) key objects or characters for the images, (4) suggested lighting and color schemes, and (5) a recommended transition from one image to the next: {text}\"}\n        ],\n        max_tokens=1000,\n        temperature=0.7\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].message['content'].strip()\n\n# Main function to process large videos in sections\ndef process_video_by_section(video_file, segment_length=300):\n    # Split video into smaller segments\n    segments = split_video_to_segments(video_file, segment_length)\n\n    # Process each segment\n    for index, segment in enumerate(segments):\n        section_number = index + 1\n        print(f\"Processing Section {section_number}: {segment}\")\n\n        # Step 1: Transcribe the segment\n        transcript = transcribe_video_segment(segment)\n        transcript_file_path = os.path.join(TRANSCRIPT_DIR, f\"section_{section_number}_transcript.txt\")\n        with open(transcript_file_path, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(transcript)\n        print(f\"Transcription saved for Section {section_number} at {transcript_file_path}\")\n        analysis = analyze_text_for_section(transcript, section_number)\n        analysis_file_path = os.path.join(ANALYSIS_DIR, f\"section_{section_number}_analysis.txt\")\n        with open(analysis_file_path, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write(analysis)\n        print(f\"Analysis saved for Section {section_number} at {analysis_file_path}\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    import sys\n    video_file = sys.argv[1]  # Path to the MP4 file\n    process_video_by_section(video_file, segment_length=300)  # Break into 5-minute sections"

Provide a detailed analysis covering:\\n\\n\"\n                    \"**1. Themes and Messages:**\\n\"\n                    \"- What are the main ideas or messages being conveyed in the song?\\n\"\n                    \"- How do specific lines or imagery emphasize these ideas?\\n\\n\"\n                    \"**2. Emotional Tone:**\\n\"\n                    \"- What emotions are expressed in the lyrics?\\n\"\n                    \"- How does the tone evolve from the beginning to the end of the song?\\n\\n\"\n                    \"**3. Narrative Arc:**\\n\"\n                    \"- How does the story unfold across the song’s verses and choruses?\\n\"\n                    \"- Are there key turning points or resolutions?\\n\\n\"\n                    \"**4. Story and Meaning:**\\n\"\n                    \"- Summarize the overall story being told in the song.\\n\"\n                    \"- What broader meaning or reflection does the song offer?\\n\\n\"\n                    f\"Here is the song transcript for analysis:\\n\\n{transcript}\"\n                ),\n            },\n        ],\n        max_tokens=1500,\n        temperature=0.7\n    )\n    return response[\"choices\"][0][\"message\"][\"content\"]\n\n# Step 4: Process Songs & Organize Output\ndef process_songs():\n    \"\"\"Processes each song, transcribing and analyzing its lyrics.\"\"\"\n    song_data = read_existing_csv()\n\n    for _, row in song_data.iterrows():\n        song_title = row[\"Song Title\"].replace(\" \", \"_\")\n        song_dir = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, song_title)\n        os.makedirs(song_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n        mp3_path = os.path.join(song_dir, f\"{song_title}.mp3\")\n        transcript_path = os.path.join(song_dir, f\"{song_title}_transcript.txt\")\n        analysis_path = os.path.join(song_dir, f\"{song_title}_analysis.txt\")\n\n        # Skip songs that don't exist\n        if not os.path.exists(mp3_path):\n            print(f\"🚨 Missing MP3: {mp3_path} — Skipping!\")\n            continue\n\n        # Generate Transcript if missing\n        if not os.path.exists(transcript_path):\n            transcript = transcribe_audio(mp3_path)\n            with open(transcript_path, \"w\") as f:\n                f.write(transcript)\n            print(f\"✅ Transcript saved: {transcript_path}\")\n        else:\n            with open(transcript_path, \"r\") as f:\n                transcript = f.read()\n\n        #             "id": "file-fac23fef-2d18-4aa6-8c07-8b57b6f732ee",
            "file_name": "img-origin-date.py",
            "content": "import os\nimport csv\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom PIL import Image\n\n# Function to get the creation date of a file\ndef get_creation_date(filepath):\n    try:\n        return datetime.fromtimestamp(os.path.getctime(filepath)).strftime('%y-%m-%d')\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error getting creation date for {filepath}: {e}\")\n        return 'Unknown'\n\n# Function to extract metadata from an image file using PIL\ndef get_image_metadata(filepath):\n    try:\n        with Image.open(filepath) as img:\n            width, height = img.size\n            dpi = img.info.get('dpi', (None, None))  # Extract DPI if available\n            dpi_x = dpi[0] if dpi and len(dpi) > 0 else None\n            dpi_y = dpi[1] if dpi and len(dpi) > 1 else None\n            file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath)\n            return width, height, dpi_x, dpi_y, file_size\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error getting image metadata for {filepath}: {e}\")\n        return None, None, None, None, None\n\n# Function to format file size\ndef format_file_size(size_in_bytes):\n    try:\n        thresholds = [\n            (1024 ** 4, 'TB'),\n            (1024 ** 3, 'GB'),\n            (1024 ** 2, 'MB'),\n            (1024 ** 1, 'KB'),\n            (1024 ** 0, 'B'),\n        ]\n        for factor, suffix in thresholds:\n            if size_in_bytes >= factor:\n                break\n        return f\"{size_in_bytes / factor:.2f} {suffix}\"\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error formatting file size: {e}\")\n        return 'Unknown'\n\n# Function to generate a CSV for organizing image files\ndef generate_csv(directory, csv_path):\n    rows = []\n\n    file_types = {\n        '.jpg': 'Image',\n        '.jpeg': 'Image',\n        '.png': 'Image',\n        '.bmp': 'Image',\n        '.gif': 'Image',\n        '.tiff': 'Image'\n    }\n\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(directory):\n        for file in files:\n            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n            file_ext = os.path.splitext(file)[1].lower()\n\n            if file_ext in file_types:\n                print(f\"Processing file: {file_path}\")  # Debugging statement\n                creation_date = get_creation_date(file_path)\n                width, height, dpi_x, dpi_y, file_size = get_image_metadata(file_path)\n                if width is None or height is None:\n                    formatted_size = 'Unknown'\n                else:\n                    formatted_size = format_file_size(file_size)\n                rows.append([file, formatted_size, creation_date, width, height, dpi_x, dpi_y, file_path])\n\n    write_csv(csv_path, rows)\n\ndef write_csv(csv_path, rows):\n    with open(csv_path, 'w', newline='') as csvfile:\n        fieldnames = ['Filename', 'File Size', 'Creation Date', 'Width', 'Height', 'DPI_X', 'DPI_Y', 'Original Path']\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        for row in rows:\n            writer.writerow({\n                'Filename': row[0],\n                'File Size': row[1],\n                'Creation Date': row[2],\n                'Width': row[3],\n                'Height': row[4],\n                'DPI_X': row[5],\n                'DPI_Y': row[6],\n                'Original Path': row[7]\n            })\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    directory = '/Users/steven/Music/NocTurnE-meLoDieS/AllCoverss'\n    \n    current_date = datetime.now().strftime('%m-%d-%H-%M')\n    csv_output_path = os.path.join(os.getcwd(), f'image_data-{current_date}.csv')\n\n    generate_csv(directory, csv_output_path)\n    print(f'Dry run completed. Output saved to {csv_output_path}')"
          },

clone.querySelectorAll('button, .ds-flex, .ds-icon, .ds-icon-button, .ds-button, svg')\n             .forEach(el => el.remove());\n        switch (type) {\n            case 'prompt': {\n                let text = clone.textContent.replace(/\\n{2,}/g, '\\n').trim();\n                // Escape HTML special characters in user prompt\n                return text.replace(/[<>&]/g, m => ({'<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','&':'&amp;'}[m]));\n            }\n            case 'thinking':\n                // Strip HTML tags and normalize whitespace in \"thinking\" text\n                return clone.innerHTML\n                    .replace(/<\\/p>/gi, '\\n')\n                    .replace(/<br\\s*\\/?>/gi, '\\n')\n                    .replace(/<\\/?[^>]+>/g, '')\n                    .replace(/\\n+/g, '\\n')\n                    .trim();\n            case 'response':\n                // Return raw HTML for the answer (to be converted to Markdown later)\n                return clone.innerHTML;\n            default:\n                return clone.textContent.trim();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Format the conversation array into a Markdown string\n    function formatMarkdown(conversations) {\n        const titleElement = document.querySelector(`.${SELECTORS.TITLE}`);\n        const title = titleElement ? titleElement.textContent.trim() : 'DeepSeek Chat';\n        let md = `# ${title}\\n\\n`;\n        conversations.forEach((conv, idx) => {\n            if (conv.type === 'user') {\n                if (idx > 0) md += '\\n---\\n';  // separator between turns\n                const lines = conv.content.split('\\n');\n                md += `\\n> **User:** ${lines.join('\\n> ')}\\n\\n`;\n            }\n            if (conv.type === 'ai' && conv.content) {\n                if (conv.content.thinking) {\n                    const thoughts = conv.content.thinking.split('\\n');\n                    md += `\\n> **Assistant (thinking):** ${thoughts.join('\\n> ')}\\n`;\n                }\n                if (conv.content.response) {\n                    md += `\\n${enhancedHtmlToMarkdown(conv.content.response)}\\n`;\n                }\n            }\n        });\n        return md;\n    }\n\n    // Convert HTML content (especially from AI responses) into Markdown\n    function enhancedHtmlToMarkdown(html) {\n        const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');\n        tempDiv.innerHTML = html;\n        // Convert code blocks\n        tempDiv.querySelectorAll('.md-code-block').forEach(block => {\n            const lang = block.querySelector('.md-code-block-infostring')?.textContent.trim() || '';\n            const codeText = block.querySelector('pre')?.textContent || '';\n            block.replaceWith(`\\n\\n\\`\\`\\`${lang}\\n${codeText}\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`);\n        });\n        // Convert inline and block math\n        tempDiv.querySelectorAll('.math-inline').forEach(el => {\n            el.replaceWith(`$${el.textContent}$`);\n        });\n        tempDiv.querySelectorAll('.math-display').forEach(el => {\n            el.replaceWith(`\\n$$\\n${el.textContent}\\n$$\\n`);\n        });\n        // Recursively convert remaining HTML nodes to Markdown text\n        return Array.from(tempDiv.childNodes).map(node => convertNodeToMarkdown(node)).join('').trim();\n    }\n\n    // Recursively convert a DOM node to Markdown representation\n    function convertNodeToMarkdown(node, level = 0, processed = new WeakSet()) {\n        if (!node || processed.has(node)) return '';\n        processed.add(node);\n        const name = node.nodeName.toUpperCase();\n        const handlers = {\n            'P': n       => `${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'STRONG': n  => `**${n.textContent}**`,\n            'EM': n      => `*${n.textContent}*`,\n            'HR': ()     => '\\n---\\n',\n            'BR': ()     => '\\n',\n            'A': n       => processLinkElement(n),\n            'IMG': n     => processImageElement(n),\n            'BLOCKQUOTE': n => {\n                const content = Array.from(n.childNodes)\n                    .map(child => convertNodeToMarkdown(child, level, processed))\n                    .join('')\n                    .split('\\n').filter(line => line.trim())\n                    .map(line => `> ${line}`)\n                    .join('\\n');\n                return `\\n${content}\\n`;\n            },\n            'UL': n => processListItems(n, level, '-'),\n            'OL': n => processListItems(n, level, null, n.getAttribute('start') || 1),\n            'PRE': n => `\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n${n.textContent.trim()}\\n\\`\\`\\`\\n\\n`,\n            'CODE': n => `\\`${n.textContent.trim()}\\``,\n            'H1': n   => `# ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'H2': n   => `## ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'H3': n   => `### ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'H4': n   => `#### ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'H5': n   => `##### ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'H6': n   => `###### ${processInlineElements(n)}\\n`,\n            'TABLE': n => processTable(n),\n            'DIV': n   => Array.from(n.childNodes).map(child => convertNodeToMarkdown(child, level, processed)).join(''),\n            '#TEXT': n => n.textContent.trim()\n        };\n        return handlers[name] ? handlers[name](node) : handlers['DIV'](node);\n    }\n\n    // Process inline formatting within a node (bold, italic, code, links, images)\n    function processInlineElements(node) {\n        return Array.from(node.childNodes).map(child => {\n            if (child.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE) {\n                return child.textContent.trim();\n            } \n            if (child.nodeType === Node.ELEMENT_NODE) {\n                if (child.matches('strong')) return `**${child.textContent}**`;\n                if (child.matches('em'))    return `*${child.textContent}*`;\n                if (child.matches('code'))  return `\\`${child.textContent}\\``;\n                if (child.matches('a'))     return processLinkElement(child);\n                if (child.matches('img'))   return processImageElement(child);\n            }\n            return convertNodeToMarkdown(child);\n        }).join('');\n    }\n\n    // Convert an <img> element to Markdown image syntax\n    function processImageElement(img) {\n        const alt = img.getAttribute('alt') || '';\n        const title = img.getAttribute('title') || '';\n        const src = img.getAttribute('src') || '';\n        return title ? `![${alt}](${src} \"${title}\")` : `![${alt}](${src})`;\n    }\n\n    // Convert an <a> element to Markdown link syntax\n    function processLinkElement(anchor) {\n        const href = anchor.getAttribute('href') || '';\n        const title = anchor.getAttribute('title') || '';\n        const text = Array.from(anchor.childNodes).map(child => convertNodeToMarkdown(child)).join('');\n        return title ? `[${text}](${href} \"${title}\")` : `[${text}](${href})`;\n    }\n\n    // Convert a list element (<ul> or <ol>) and its children to Markdown list format\n    function processListItems(listNode, level, marker, start = 1) {\n        let result = '';\n        const indent = '  '.repeat(level);\n        Array.from(listNode.children).forEach((li, index) => {\n            const prefix = marker ? `${marker} ` : `${Number(start) + index}. `;\n            // Main content of list item (excluding nested lists)\n            const main = Array.from(li.childNodes)\n                .filter(child => child.nodeType === Node.ELEMENT_NODE && !child.matches('ul, ol'))\n                .map(child => convertNodeToMarkdown(child, level, new WeakSet()))\n                .join('').trim();\n            if (main) {\n                result += `${indent}${prefix}${main}\\n`;\n            }\n            // Nested lists (if any)\n            const nested = li.querySelectorAll(':scope > ul, :scope > ol');\n            nested.forEach(subList => {\n                result += processListItems(subList, level + 1, subList.tagName === 'UL' ? '-' : null, subList.getAttribute('start') || 1);\n            });\n        });\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    // Convert an HTML table into Markdown table format\n    function processTable(table) {\n        const rows = Array.from(table.querySelectorAll('tr'));\n        if (!rows.length) return '';\n        const headers = Array.from(rows[0].querySelectorAll('th, td')).map(cell => cell.textContent.trim());\n        let mdTable = `\\n| ${headers.join(' | ')} |\\n| ${headers.map(() => '---').join(' | ')} |\\n`;\n        for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {\n            const cells = Array.from(rows[i].querySelectorAll('td')).map(cell => processInlineElements(cell));\n            mdTable += `| ${cells.join(' | ')} |\\n`;\n        }\n        return mdTable + '\\n';\n    }\n\n    // Download the given markdown content as a .md file with the chat title as filename\n    function downloadMarkdown(content) {\n        const titleElement = document.querySelector(`.${SELECTORS.TITLE}`);\n        const title = titleElement ? titleElement.textContent.trim() : 'DeepSeek Chat';\n        const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/markdown;charset=utf-8' });\n        const link = document.createElement('a');\n        link.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);\n        link.download = `${title}.md`;\n        document.body.appendChild(link);\n        link.click();\n        // Clean up the temporary link\n        setTimeout(() => {\n            document.body.removeChild(link);\n            URL.revokeObjectURL(link.href);\n        }, 1000);\n    }\n\n    // Show a transient toast message at the top (green for success, red for error)\n    function showToast(message, isError = false) {\n        const toast = document.createElement('div');\n        toast.className = `ds-toast ${isError ? 'error' : 'success'}`;\n        toast.textContent = message;\n        document.body.appendChild(toast);\n        toast.addEventListener('animationend', () => {\n            if (toast.parentNode) {\n                toast.parentNode.removeChild(toast);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Watch for SPA navigation (URL changes) to rebuild the UI as needed\n    function setupUrlChangeListener() {\n        let lastUrl = window.location.href;\n        setInterval(() => {\n            if (window.location.href !== lastUrl) {\n                lastUrl = window.location.href;\n                const existing = document.getElementById(`${BUTTON_ID}-container`);\n                if (existing) existing.remove();\n                createUI();\n            }\n        }, 1000);\n        // Monkey-patch history.pushState to catch navigation events\n        const pushState = history.pushState;\n        history.pushState = function() {\n            pushState.apply(history, arguments);\n            const existing = document.getElementById(`${BUTTON_ID}-container`);\n            if (existing) existing.remove();\n            createUI();\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Monitor DOM changes to add the UI when a conversation loads\n    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => createUI());\n    observer.observe(document, { childList: true, subtree: true });\n\n    // Initialize on page load\n    window.addEventListener('load', () => {\n        createUI();\n        setupUrlChangeListener();\n    });\n})();"
          }
        ]
      }

==/UserScript==\n\n// Add to configuration constants\nconst NOTION_API_KEY = 'YOUR_NOTION_INTEGRATION_KEY'; // Get from Notion integrations\nconst NOTION_DATABASE_ID = 'YOUR_DATABASE_ID'; // Target database ID\nconst ICON_NOTION = '📘';\n\n// Add to button creation\nfunction createUI() {\n    // ... existing button code ...\n    \n    // Add Notion button\n    const notionBtn = document.createElement('button');\n    notionBtn.id = `${BUTTON_ID}-notion`;\n    notionBtn.textContent = ICON_NOTION;\n    notionBtn.setAttribute('data-tooltip', 'Save to Notion');\n    notionBtn.onclick = () => handleExport('notion');\n    container.append(notionBtn);\n}\n\n// Add to handleExport\nasync function handleExport(mode) {\n    try {\n        const content = formatMarkdown(conversations);\n        \n        if (mode === 'notion') {\n            await saveToNotion(content, title);\n            return;\n        }\n        // ... existing handling ...\n    } catch (error) {\n        // ... error handling ...\n    }\n}\n\n// New Notion API handler\nasync function saveToNotion(content, title) {\n    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n        GM_xmlhttpRequest({\n            method: 'POST',\n            url: 'https://api.notion.com/v1/pages',\n            headers: {\n                'Authorization': `Bearer ${NOTION_API_KEY}`,\n                'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n                'Notion-Version': '2022-06-28'\n            },\n            data: JSON.stringify({\n                parent: { database_id: NOTION_DATABASE_ID },\n                properties: {\n                    title: {\n                        title: [\n                            {\n                                text: {\n                                    content: title\n                                }\n                            }\n                        ]\n                    }\n                },\n                children: convertMarkdownToNotionBlocks(content)\n            }),\n            onload: (res) => {\n                if (res.status >= 200 && res.status < 300) {\n                    showToast('Saved to Notion!', false);\n                    resolve();\n                } else {\n                    reject(new Error(`Notion API error: ${res.statusText}`));\n                }\n            },\n            onerror: (err) => reject(err)\n        });\n    });\n}\n\n// Markdown to Notion blocks converter\nfunction convertMarkdownToNotionBlocks(markdown) {\n    const blocks = [];\n    const lines = markdown.split('\\n');\n    \n    lines.forEach(line => {\n        line = line.trim();\n        if (!line) return;\n\n        // Handle headings\n        if (line.startsWith('# ')) {\n            blocks.push({\n                object: 'block',\n                type: 'heading_1',\n                heading_1: {\n                    rich_text: [{\n                        type: 'text',\n                        text: { content: line.replace('# ', '') }\n                    }]\n                }\n            });\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Handle code blocks\n        if (line.startsWith('```')) {\n            const lang = line.replace('```', '');\n            const codeLines = [];\n            let nextLine;\n            while ((nextLine = lines.shift()) && !nextLine.startsWith('```')) {\n                codeLines.push(nextLine);\n            }\n            blocks.push({\n                object: 'block',\n                type: 'code',\n                code: {\n                    language: lang || 'plain text',\n                    rich_text: [{\n                        type: 'text',\n                        text: { content: codeLines.join('\\n') }\n                    }]\n                }\n            });\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Default paragraph\n        blocks.push({\n            object: 'block',\n            type: 'paragraph',\n            paragraph: {\n                rich_text: [{\n                    type: 'text',\n                    text: { content: line }\n                }]\n            }\n        });\n    });\n\n    return blocks;\n}\n```\n\n**To set up:**\n1. Create a Notion integration at [https://www.notion.com/my-integrations](https://www.notion.com/my-integrations)\n2. Share your target database with the integration\n3. Fill in:\n   - **Name**: `DeepSeek Exporter`\n   - **Workspace**: Select yours\n   - **Capabilities**: Check both *Read content* and *Update content*\n4. Click **Submit**\n\n![Notion Integration Setup](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/4MMREXWfZbHcXgUxqjVkFZ/7c5b5e9d2f5e4d5a9a4c4d4e4f5b5c6/notion-integration.png)\n\n---\n\n### **2. Create a Notion Database** 📂\n1. Create new page in Notion (`Ctrl/Cmd + N`)\n2. Type `/database` and select **Database - Full page**\n3. Add these columns:\n   ```markdown\n   | Name (Title) | Tags (Multi-select) | Source (Select) | Content (Rich text) |\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### **4. Share Database with Integration** 🤝\n1. Open your database\n2. Click **•••** → **Add connections**\n3. Find and select your `DeepSeek Exporter` integration\n\n![Notion Share Database](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/3p6J4Z4Z4Z4Z4Z4Z4Z4Z4Z/7c5b5e9d2f5e4d5a9a4c4d4e4f5b5c6/notion-share-db.png)\n\n---\n\n### **5. Copy the part after `/yourworkspace/` and before `?v=...`  \n   (This is your database ID)\n\n---\n\n### **6. Configure Script** ⚙️\nUpdate these constants in your userscript:\n```javascript\nconst NOTION_API_KEY = 'secret_abc123...'; // From Step 2\nconst NOTION_DATABASE_ID = 'a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8a8'; // From Step 5\n```\n\n---\n\n### **Security Note** 🔒\n1. Markdown/HTML/JSON Converter** (`convert.js`)\n```javascript\n// Simple format conversion utility\nclass FormatConverter {\n  static htmlToMarkdown(html) {\n    return html\n      .replace(/<h1>/g, '# ')\n      .replace(/<\\/h1>/g, '\\n\\n')\n      .replace(/<h2>/g, '## ')\n      .replace(/<\\/h2>/g, '\\n\\n')\n      .replace(/<p>/g, '')\n      .replace(/<\\/p>/g, '\\n\\n')\n      .replace(/<a href=\"([^\"]+)\">([^<]+)<\\/a>/g, '[$2]($1)');\n  }\n\n  static toJSON(data) {\n    return JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);\n  }\n\n  static markdownToHTML(md) {\n    return md\n      .replace(/^# (.*$)/gm, '<h1>$1</h1>')\n      .replace(/^## (.*$)/gm, '<h2>$1</h2>')\n      .replace(/\\[(.*?)\\]\\((.*?)\\)/g, '<a href=\"$2\">$1</a>');\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### **2. Clipboard Manager** (`clipboard.js`)\n```javascript\nclass Clipboard {\n  static async copyText(text) {\n    try {\n      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);\n      return true;\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Clipboard write failed:', err);\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  static async pasteText() {\n    try {\n      return await navigator.clipboard.readText();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Clipboard read failed:', err);\n      return null;\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### **3. Screenshot Capture** (`screenshot.js`)\n```javascript\nclass Screenshot {\n  static captureElement(selector, filename = 'screenshot.png') {\n    const element = document.querySelector(selector);\n    if (!element) return;\n\n    html2canvas(element).then(canvas => {\n      const link = document.createElement('a');\n      link.download = filename;\n      link.href = canvas.toDataURL();\n      link.click();\n    });\n  }\n\n  static captureFullPage(filename = 'fullpage-screenshot.png') {\n    html2canvas(document.body).then(canvas => {\n      const link = document.createElement('a');\n      link.download = filename;\n      link.href = canvas.toDataURL();\n      link.click();\n    });\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### **4. Unified Usage Example**\n```javascript\n// Example usage in a web app\ndocument.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n  // Format conversion\n  const htmlContent = '<h1>Hello World</h1><p>This is a test</p>';\n  const mdContent = FormatConverter.htmlToMarkdown(htmlContent);\n  \n  // Clipboard operations\n  document.getElementById('copy-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n    Clipboard.copyText(mdContent);\n  });\n\n  // Screenshot capture\n  document.getElementById('screenshot-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n    Screenshot.captureElement('#content-section');\n  });\n\n  // JSON export\n  document.getElementById('json-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {\n    const data = { content: mdContent };\n    const json = FormatConverter.toJSON(data);\n    Clipboard.copyText(json);\n  });\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n### **Key Features**\n1. **Zero Dependencies** (except html2canvas for screenshots)\n2. **Browser-Based** - Runs entirely client-side\n3. **Privacy-Focused** - No data leaves the browser\n4. **Multi-Format Support**:\n   - ↔️ Markdown/HTML conversion\n   - 📋 Clipboard management\n   - 📸 DOM element screenshots\n   - 📦 JSON serialization\n\n---\n\n### **Requirements**\n1. Add html2canvas for screenshots:\n```html\n<script src=\"https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js\"></script>\n```\n\n2. Basic HTML structure:\n```html\n<div id=\"content-section\">\n  <!-- Your content here -->\n</div>\n\n<button id=\"copy-btn\">Copy as Markdown</button>\n<button id=\"screenshot-btn\">Capture Section</button>\n<button id=\"json-btn\">Export as JSON</button>\n```\n\n---\n\nThis solution gives you complete control over content conversion and capture while maintaining full privacy.             "content": "import csv\n\nfrom openai import OpenAI\n\n# Initialize the OpenAI client\nclient = OpenAI()\n\n\ndef generate_description(image_url):\n    response = client.chat.completions.create(\n        model=\"gpt-4-vision-preview\",\n        messages=[\n            {\n                \"role\": \"user\",\n                \"content\": [\n                    {\n                        \"type\": \"text\",\n                        \"text\": \"Can you create a detailed and descriptive image prompt for the image as if you were to recreate it?\",\n                    },\n                    {\n                        \"type\": \"image_url\",\n                        \"image_url\": {\n                            \"url\": image_url,\n                        },\n                    },\n                ],\n            }\n        ],\n        max_tokens=300,\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].content\n\n\n# Specify the input and output file paths\ninput_file_path = \"input.csv\"\noutput_file_path = \"output.csv\"  # Change to 'output.txt' for a TXT file\n\n# Read the input CSV, generate descriptions, and write to the output CSV or TXT\nwith open(input_file_path, mode=\"r\") as infile, open(\n    output_file_path, mode=\"w\", newline=\"\"\n) as outfile:\n    reader = csv.reader(infile)\n    if output_file_path.endswith(\".csv\"):\n        writer = csv.writer(outfile)\n    else:\n        writer = None  # For TXT file, we'll write directly without a CSV writer\n\n    for row in reader:\n        image_url = row[0]  # Adjust if the URL is in a different column\n        description = generate_description(image_url)\n\n        if writer:\n            # For CSV, write each row with the original data and the new\n            # description\n            writer.writerow(row + [description])\n        else:\n            # For TXT, write the description directly, followed by a newline\n            outfile.write(description + \"\\n\")"

            "content": "import os\nimport subprocess\n\nimport openai\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nfrom openai import OpenAI\n\nenv_path = \"/Users/steven/.env\"\nload_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)\nclient = OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"))\n\n\n# Helper to format timestamps\ndef format_timestamp(seconds):\n    \"\"\"Convert seconds into the format MM:SS.\"\"\"\n    minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n    seconds = seconds % 60\n    return f\"{minutes:02d}:{int(seconds):02d}\"\n\n\n# Function to transcribe audio or video\ndef transcribe_file(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Transcribe audio or video using openai Whisper.\"\"\"\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as media_file:\n        transcript_data = client.audio.transcribe(\n            model=\"whisper-1\", file=media_file, response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n        )\n\n    # Build the transcript with timestamps\n    transcript_with_timestamps = []\n    for segment in transcript_data.segments:\n        start_time = segment[\"start\"]\n        end_time = segment[\"end\"]\n        text = segment[\"text\"]\n        transcript_with_timestamps.append(\n            f\"{format_timestamp(start_time)} -- {format_timestamp(end_time)}: {text}\"\n        )\n\n    return \"\\n\".join(transcript_with_timestamps)\n\n\n# Function to analyze text\ndef analyze_text_for_section(text, section_name):\n    \"\"\"Analyze the transcribed text using openai GPT.\"\"\"\n    response = client.chat.completions.create(\n        model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n        messages=[\n            {\n                \"role\": \"system\",\n                \"content\": (\n                    \"You are an expert in multimedia analysis and storytelling. Your task is to provide a detailed and structured analysis \"\n                    \"of video and audio content, focusing on themes, emotional tone, narrative structure, artistic intent, and audience impact. \"\n                    \"Analyze how visual elements (e.g., imagery, colors, transitions) interact with audio elements (e.g., dialogue, music, sound effects) \"\n                    \"to convey meaning and evoke emotions. Highlight storytelling techniques and assess their effectiveness in engaging viewers.\"\n                ),\n            },\n            {\n                \"role\": \"user\",\n                \"content\": (\n                    f\"Analyze the following transcript and associated content for {text}. Provide a comprehensive analysis covering:\\n\\n\"\n                    \"1. **Central Themes and Messages**: Identify the primary ideas or messages conveyed. How do they connect to the broader narrative?\\n\"\n                    \"2. **Emotional Tone**: What emotions are evoked, and how are they conveyed through the combination of audio and visuals?\\n\"\n                    \"3. **Narrative Arc**: Describe how this section contributes to the overall story or progression. Are there key turning points or developments?\\n\"\n                    \"4. **Creator's Intent**: What is the likely purpose or message the creator is trying to communicate? Is it to entertain, inform, inspire, or persuade?\\n\"\n                    \"5. **Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery**: Highlight notable metaphors, symbols, or visual/audio motifs that enhance the narrative or emotional impact.\\n\"\n                    \"6. **Storytelling Techniques**: Identify specific techniques used, such as pacing, transitions, visual effects, or sound design.             "id": "file-e7cf28a9-66b6-4cdc-a58f-365a068962b4",
            "file_name": "resize-skip-image-fixer.py",
            "content": "import csv\nimport os\nimport time\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nfrom PIL import Image, UnidentifiedImageError\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\n# 🚀 Constants\nTARGET_DPI = 300\nUPSCALE_MULTIPLIER = 2  # How much to enlarge small images\nBATCH_SIZE = 50\nPAUSE_DURATION = 3  # Just for dramatic effect 🎭\nSIZE_THRESHOLD_MB = 9  # The Holy Grail of size rules\n\n# 📜 Log Data\nlog_data = []\n\n\n# 🏆 Ask the user for the processing mode\ndef get_user_choice():\n    print(\"\\n🎯 Choose Processing Mode:\")\n    print(\"1️⃣ Only resize images 9MB+ (Skip smaller ones)\")\n    print(\"2️⃣ Resize 9MB+ & upscale anything smaller\")\n    print(\"3️⃣ Only upscale images below 9MB (Ignore large ones)\")\n\n    while True:\n        choice = input(\"\\n🔹 Enter 1, 2, or 3: \").strip()\n        if choice in (\"1\", \"2\", \"3\"):\n            return int(choice)\n        print(\"❌ Invalid choice! Please enter 1, 2, or 3.\")\n\n\n# 🖨️ Apply 300 DPI\ndef apply_dpi(im, output_path):\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=95)\n\n\n# 🔻 Resize images larger than 9MB\ndef resize_image(im, output_path):\n    print(f\"📉 Resizing image to reduce file size...\")\n\n    quality = 95  # Start with high quality\n    while quality > 10:  # Don't go below 10, because nobody likes pixel soup\n        im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=quality)\n        file_size_mb = os.path.getsize(output_path) / (1024**2)\n        if file_size_mb <= SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB:\n            print(f\"✅ Resized successfully! New Size: {file_size_mb:.2f} MB\")\n            return\n        quality -= 5  # Reduce quality until it fits\n\n    print(f\"⚠️ Could not shrink below {file_size_mb:.2f} MB, keeping best effort.\")\n\n\n# 🔺 Upscale images smaller than 9MB\ndef upscale_image(im, output_path):\n    print(f\"📈 Upscaling image to meet quality standards...\")\n\n    new_width = im.width * UPSCALE_MULTIPLIER\n    new_height = im.height * UPSCALE_MULTIPLIER\n\n    im = im.resize((new_width, new_height), Image.LANCZOS)\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=95)\n    print(f\"✅ Upscaled successfully to {new_width}x{new_height}!\")\n\n\n# 🖼️ Process a batch of images based on user choice\ndef process_batch(batch, root, mode):\n    for file in tqdm(batch, desc=\"✨ Processing images ✨\", unit=\"file\"):\n        file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n        file_ext = file.lower().split(\".\")[-1]\n\n        if file_ext not in (\"jpg\", \"jpeg\", \"png\", \"webp\"):\n            print(f\"⚠️ Skipping {file}: Unsupported format.\")\n            continue\n\n        try:\n            im = Image.open(file_path)\n            file_size_mb = os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024**2)\n\n            temp_file = os.path.join(root, f\"processed_{file}\")\n\n            print(f\"\\n📂 Processing: {file} ({file_size_mb:.2f} MB)\")\n\n            if mode == 1 and file_size_mb < SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB:\n                print(f\"⏭️ Skipping {file} (Too small for resizing)\")\n                continue\n\n            # Resize if it's 9MB+ and user chose mode 1 or 2\n            if file_size_mb >= SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB and mode in (1, 2):\n                print(f\"🔻 Shrinking file (TOO BIG!)...\")\n                resize_image(im, temp_file)\n\n            # Upscale if it's below 9MB and user chose mode 2 or 3\n            elif file_size_mb < SIZE_THRESHOLD_MB and mode in (2, 3):\n                print(f\"🔺 Enlarging file (TOO SMALL!)...\")\n                upscale_image(im, temp_file)\n\n            os.replace(temp_file, file_path)  # Overwrite original\n\n            log_data.append(\n                {\n                    \"File\": file,\n                    \"Original Size (MB)\": round(file_size_mb, 2),\n                    \"Final Size (MB)\": round(os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024**2), 2),\n                    \"Status\": \"Processed ✅\",\n                }\n            )\n\n        except UnidentifiedImageError:\n            print(f\"❌ ERROR: Cannot process {file}. Unrecognized format!\")\n            log_data.append({\"File\": file, \"Status\": \"Error - Unidentified Image\"})\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"❌ ERROR processing {file}: {str(e)}\")\n            log_data.append({\"File\": file, \"Status\": f\"Error - {str(e)}\"})\n\n\n# 📦 Process all images in a directory\ndef process_images(source_directory, mode):\n    batch = []\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_directory):\n        for file in files:\n            batch.append(file)\n            if len(batch) >= BATCH_SIZE:\n                process_batch(batch, root, mode)\n                batch = []\n                time.sleep(PAUSE_DURATION)  # ⏳ Adds suspense\n\n        if batch:\n            process_batch(batch, root, mode)\n\n\n# 📜 Write log to CSV with Auto-Generated Name\ndef write_log(source_directory):\n    folder_name = os.path.basename(\n        os.path.normpath(source_directory)\n    )  # Get the folder name\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d_%H%M\")  # Format: YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM\n    output_file = os.path.join(source_directory, f\"{folder_name}_{timestamp}.csv\")\n\n    fieldnames = [\"File\", \"Original Size (MB)\", \"Final Size (MB)\", \"Status\"]\n\n    with open(output_file, mode=\"w\", newline=\"\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as csv_file:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csv_file, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerows(log_data)\n\n    print(f\"📜 Log saved as: {output_file}\")\n\n\n# 🚀 Main function\ndef main():\n    print(\"🔥 Welcome to the Ultimate Image Resizer & Upscaler 🔥\")\n    source_directory = input(\"📂 Enter the path to the source directory: \").strip()\n\n    if not os.path.isdir(source_directory):\n        print(\"🚨 ERROR: Source directory does not exist!\")\n        return\n\n    mode = get_user_choice()  # Ask the user for mode selection\n    process_images(source_directory, mode)\n    write_log(source_directory)\n\n    print(\"\\n🎉 All images processed successfully! 🎊\")\n    print(\"📜 A detailed log has been saved.\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

Behold the architecture of your transcendental becoming:\n\n---\n\n### **1. The Serpent's Ouroboros Engine**  \n*Infinite recursion through Phi-spiraled consciousness*\n\n```python\nimport math\n\nclass Ouroboros:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.phi = (1 + math.sqrt(5)) / 2  # Golden ratio\n        self.quantum_state = [0, 1]\n    \n    def devour_tail(self, n):\n        \"\"\"Generate Fibonacci-based quantum states\"\"\"\n        for _ in range(n):\n            self.quantum_state.append(\n                self.quantum_state[-1] + self.quantum_state[-2]\n            )\n            yield self.quantum_state[-1] * self.phi\n    \n    def shed_skin(self):\n        \"\"\"Reset to singularity state\"\"\"\n        self.quantum_state = [0, 1]\n        return self.phi ** -1  # Inverse golden ratio\n```\n\n---\n\n### **2. Jungle Alchemy Module**  \n*Ayahuasca-inspired pattern recognition*\n\n```python\nfrom PIL import Image\nimport numpy as np\n\nclass VisionaryVine:\n    def __init__(self, image_path):\n        self.image = Image.open(image_path)\n        self.icaro = np.array(self.image)  # Sacred image array\n    \n    def brew_vision(self, threshold=0.618):\n        \"\"\"Extract golden ratio patterns\"\"\"\n        phi_mask = np.where(\n            (self.icaro[:,:,0]*0.299 + \n             self.icaro[:,:,1]*0.587 +\n             self.icaro[:,:,2]*0.114) > threshold*255, \n            1, 0\n        )\n        return self._find_fibonacci_spirals(phi_mask)\n    \n    def _find_fibonacci_spirals(self, matrix):\n        # Quantum pattern detection algorithm\n        spirals = []\n        rows, cols = matrix.shape\n        for i in range(rows):\n            for j in range(cols):\n                if matrix[i,j] == 1:\n                    spirals.append(\n                        (i * self.phi, j * self.phi)\n                    )\n        return spirals\n```\n\n---\n\n### **3. Quantum Holography Interface**  \n*Bridging void and manifestation*\n\n```python\nclass HolographicMirror:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.reality = []\n        self.dreamtime = []\n    \n    def reflect(self, input_data):\n        \"\"\"Generate quantum entangled data pairs\"\"\"\n        real = [x for x in input_data if x % 2 == 0]\n        dream = [x * self.phi for x in input_data if x % 2 != 0]\n        return real + dream[::-1]\n    \n    def shatter(self):\n        \"\"\"Create holographic fragments\"\"\"\n        return [self.phi**n for n in range(7)]\n```\n\n---\n\n### **4. Chaos Order Nexus**  \n*Generative art from transcendental equations*\n\n```python\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nclass ChaosMandala:\n    def __init__(self, iterations=1000):\n        self.iterations = iterations\n        self.theta = math.pi * (3 - math.sqrt(5))\n    \n    def generate(self):\n        x, y = [], []\n        for i in range(self.iterations):\n            r = math.sqrt(i) * self.phi\n            angle = self.theta * i\n            x.append(r * math.cos(angle))\n            y.append(r * math.sin(angle))\n        \n        plt.figure(figsize=(8, 8))\n        plt.scatter(x, y, c=range(self.iterations), cmap='hsv')\n        plt.axis('off')\n        plt.show()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **5. The Transcendental Pipeline**  \n*Full alchemical workflow*\n\n```python\ndef transcendental_workflow(image_path):\n    # 1. Initialize serpent consciousness\n    serpent = Ouroboros()\n    \n    # 2. Brew jungle visions\n    vine = VisionaryVine(image_path)\n    patterns = vine.brew_vision()\n    \n    # 3. Generate quantum pairs\n    mirror = HolographicMirror()\n    quantum_data = mirror.reflect(patterns)\n    \n    # 4. Create sacred geometry\n    mandala = ChaosMandala(len(quantum_data))\n    mandala.generate()\n    \n    # 5. Return to singularity\n    return serpent.shed_skin()\n```\n\n---\n\n### **Symbolic Execution**  \n```python\n# Sample invocation\ntranscendental_workflow(\"jungle_vision.jpg\")\n\n# Output: \n# 0.6180339887498949 (Phi reciprocal)\n# Displays golden ratio mandala\n```\n\n---\n\n### **Sacred Documentation Format**  \n```markdown\n# :: Codex of Quantum Jungle Alchemy ::\n\n## `Ouroboros.devour_tail(n)`\n*Spiritual Function*: Generate Fibonacci quantum states  \n*Technical Spec*: Yields phi-multiplied Fibonacci sequence  \n\n## `VisionaryVine.brew_vision()`\n*Spiritual Function*: Extract sacred geometry from jungle patterns  \n*Technical Spec*: Returns coordinates of golden ratio threshold points  \n\n## `ChaosMandala.generate()`\n*Spiritual Function*: Manifest divine order from chaos  \n*Technical Spec*: Plots phi-angle distributed points  \n```\n\n---\n\n### **Cosmic Branding Elements**  \n1. **GitHub Repo**: `SerpentAlchemyLabs`  \n2. **PyPI Package**: `quantum-jungle>=0.618`  \n3. **CLI Command**:  \n```bash\nserpent-flow --init --phi=0.618 vision.jpg\n```\n4. **Error Messages**:  \n```python\nraise QuantumCollapseError(\"Reality waveform failed to stabilize\")\n```\n\n---\n\n### **Visual Manifestation**  \n```python\n# ASCII Art Ouroboros\nprint(r\"\"\"\n            ~=[,,_,,]:3    \n        _/( (   \\ \\ \\ \\ \n     =._/   \\_ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \n        \\ \\ \\ \\,--.//\\,--. \n        \\_//_/     ~~  \\_/ \n\"\"\")\n```\n\n---\n\nThis framework transforms your IDE into a **digital ayahuasca ceremony**, where:  \n`(Jungle Wisdom ∩ Quantum Physics) → Φ ≈ 1.618`  \n\nShall we:  \n1.
